### Question 103: How many way can I fill in the requirements of EL?  
### Answer: 

There are several ways to fulfill the Experiential Learning (EL) requirements at Fulbright University Vietnam. Here's a breakdown:

1. **ELP Streams**: The Experiential Learning Program (ELP) offers various streams such as those housed within Academic Affairs (AA), Career Services (CS), and Center for Entrepreneurship and Innovation (CEI). Each stream provides different types of experiential learning opportunities, such as internships, research projects, community service, and entrepreneurial ventures. Students can enroll in these courses to earn credits towards their EL requirement.

2. **Elective Courses**: EL credits can also be earned through elective courses. Students are free to choose from a wide range of courses listed in the Course Catalogue. They can select electives that offer experiential learning components, such as lab-based science courses, studio art classes, or fieldwork in social sciences.

3. **Major Requirements**: With advisor approval, EL credits can be applied towards major requirements. This means that students can incorporate experiential learning into their major coursework, potentially fulfilling both major and EL requirements simultaneously.

4. **Capstone Pathway**: The capstone pathway, which is an optional but highly recommended part of the curriculum, can also include EL components. Students can design their capstone project to include experiential learning activities, thus earning EL credits while completing their capstone requirement.

5. **Interdisciplinary Minors**: For students pursuing a minor in a different field, courses required for the minor that include experiential learning components can also count towards the EL requirement, provided they are not already counted towards the 8-credit limit for out-of-area courses.

The total number of EL credits required is between 4 and 12 credits, and students must ensure that their chosen EL activities are approved by their academic advisor to ensure they meet the university's standards and contribute effectively to their educational journey.

It's important to note that while the ELP provides structured opportunities, students are also encouraged to seek out their own experiential learning opportunities, as long as they are approved by the university and meet the criteria for academic credit. This flexibility allows students to tailor their EL experience to their personal interests and career goals.

In summary, students can fulfill the EL requirements by participating in ELP streams, taking elective courses with experiential components, applying EL credits to their major requirements with advisor approval, completing a capstone project with EL components, and incorporating EL into interdisciplinary minors, all while ensuring that their chosen activities are academically rigorous and aligned with their educational objectives.

While the number of elective credits may vary, the total number of earned credits must be at least 128. Electives enable students to explore different subjects across the curriculum to build a broad and diverse background or to pursue more specialized studies within their major. Alternatively, students may use electives to fulfill requirements for another minor or major. 13.6  Capstone All majors at Fulbright offer an optional capstone pathway to be completed during the student’s final year. Students may apply for

tagged. For instance, if major A requires certain courses from major B for out-of-area foundation, exploration, or applications of the major, and these courses are not cross-listed between A and B, they do not count toward the 8-credit limit. 1 In interdisciplinary minors, the requirements mainly consist of courses from other majors. These courses are usually not cross-listed with the minors and are referred to as 'tagged' by these minors. 13.4  Experiential Learning Requirements Experiential Learning can count toward elective or major requirements (upon advisor approval). Fulbright’s Experiential Learning Program (ELP) exists to create, standardize, and facilitate academic credit-bearing experiential learning experiences. All full-time, undergraduate, degree- seeking students must complete at least 04 credits and a maximum of 12 credits under the ELP as a graduation requirement. Current ELP streams are housed within Academic Affairs (AA), Career Services (CS), and Center for Entrepreneurship and Innovation
